## Source boundary
- Public MUSINSA product sitemap/product pages only.
- Crawled with User-Agent ChatGPT-User after robots.txt allow check.
- Excludes login, account, cart, order, payment, personalized, and private inventory data.
- Production should use authorized MUSINSA API/feed.
